BA'I TSOD TZAM NA RTEN 'BREL BCU GNYIS DANG BDEN BZHI SHES NAS
SKAD CIG GCIG DANG LDAN PA'I SHES RAB KYIS MNGON PAR SANGS RGYAS
SO, ,DE NAS SHING TA LA BDUN TZAM DU 'PHAGS TE

LAM GYI RGYUD NI CHAD DO ZHES PA LA SOGS PA CHED DU BRJOD PA
BRJOD DO, ,LHA RNAMS KYIS KYANG ME TOG PUS MO NUB TZAM GTOR TE
MCHOD DO, ,'JIG RTEN SNANG BAR BYAS, SA G-YOS, PHYOGS BCU'I
SANGS RGYAS KYIS CHOS KYI DGA' BA BSKUR PHYAG

BRKYANGS TE, BDAG CAG JI LTAR BYANG CHUB THOB LTAR KHYOD SANGS
RGYAS, ,DPER NA MAR DANG MAR GYI NYING KHU MTSUNGS 'DRA BZHIN,
,ZHES GSUNGS SHING LHA'I BU MO RNAMS KYIS BSTOD DO, ,STON PAS
KYANG, BSOD NAMS RNAM SMIN BDE STER SDUG BSNGAL

THAMS CAD SEL, ,BSOD NAMS LDAN PA'I MI YI BSAM PA RNAMS KYANG
'GRUB, ,BDUD BCOM NAS NI BYANG CHUB MYUR DU REG PAR 'GYUR, ,MYA
NGAN LAS 'DAS ZHI BA BSIL BA'I DNGOS PO THOB, ,CES CHED DU BRJOD
DO, ,LHA RNAMS KYIS RGYA CHER

BSTOD NAS SKYIL KRUNG MA BSHIG PAR ZHAG BDUN DU BYANG CHUB SHING
LA GZIGS SO, ,ZHAG BDUN PA GNYIS PA LA STONG GSUM RGYANG RING DU
'CHAG GO ,GSUM PA LA NGAS 'DIR SDUG BSNGAL MTHAR PHYUNG ZHES
BYANG CHUB KYI SNYING PO LA SPYAN MI

'DZUM PAR GZIGS SO, ,BZHI PA LA SHAR NUB KYI BAR DU RGYANG MI
RING PAR 'CHAG GO, ,DE NAS BDUD SDIG CAN GYIS MYA NGAN LAS 'DA'
BAR GSOL BA BTAB KYANG GDUL BYA'I DON BYAS ZIN GYI BAR DU MI
'DA' BAR ZHAL GYIS BZHES TE MYA

CHOS THOS PA DANG

MTHONG BA DANG, ,DBEN PAR DGA' BA BDE BA YIN, ,SROG CHAGS 'BYUNG
PO RNAMS LA BSDAMS, ,GNOD BA MI BYED 'JIG RTEN BDE, ,ZHES SOGS
GSUNGS SO, ,BDUN PA LA SHING SGROL RGYU'I DRUNG DU BZHUGS TE,
TSONG PA GA GON DANG BZANG POS SBRANG RTZI DANG SKYO

MA DANG BU RAM SHING BSHUS PA DAG PHUL BA DANG, LAG PAS BLANGS
NAM LEGS, SNGON GYI SANGS RGYAS KYIS SNOD JI LTA BUR BZHES SNYAM
PA DANG, RGYAL CHEN BZHIS GSER LA SOGS PA'I LHUNG BZED PHUL BA
MA BZHES PAS RNAM SRAS LA RNGON PA'I RIGS KYI LHAS BYIN

,NGA 'DRA DAG LA LHUNG BZED PHUL BA NI, ,DRAN DANG BLO GROS NAM
YANG

BA'I DKYIL 'KHOR CHO GA DGE TSUL KHYUNG GRAGS KYI 'GYUR, 'DI
RTZOD PA CAN NO,, NGAN SONG SBYONG BA'I DKYIL CHOG RIN CHEN
BZANG PO'I 'GYUR 'DI GTZUG DGU'I YIN, KHAMS GSUM RNAM

RGYAL GYI DKYIL CHOG RIN CHEN BZANG PO'I 'GYUR, SKU GZUGS SPYAN
DBYE BA'I CHO GA STE, BCU PO 'DI SLOB DPON KUN DGA' SNYING POS
MDZAD PA'O, ,SLOB DPON KUN SNYING GIS MDZAD PA'I KUN RIG GI
DKYIL 'KHOR CHO GA RIN CHEN BZANG PO'I 'GYUR, DES MDZAD PA'I

RAB GNAS KYI CHO GA RIN CHEN BZANG PO'I 'GYUR, RDO RJE SEMS DPA'
'BYUNG BA CHE BA DANG CHUNG BA GNYIS TE, BZHI MA CHUD CING CHE
BA MA RNYED DO, ,NGAN SONG SBYONG RGYUD KYI 'GREL PA SNANG BA'I
RGYAN DBANG PHYUG RGYAL MTSAN GYI 'GYUR, SLOB DPON PRADZNY'A P'A
LI TAS

MDZAD PA'I SPYAN DBYE'I CHO GA RNAMS MA TSUD, SLOB DPON SH'AKYA
BSHES GNYEN GYIS MDZAD PA'I DE NYID BSDUS PA'I RGYA CHER 'GREL
KO SA LA'I RGYAN BAM PO SUM CU PA RIN CHEN BZANG PO'I 'GYUR, RDO
RJE 'BYUNG BA'I BSDUS DON SLOB DPON MU N'INDRA BHA DRAS MJAD

PA CHOS KYI SHES RAB KYI 'GYUR, SLOB DPON RDO RJE GO CHAS MDZAD
PA'I NGAN SONG SBYONG BA'I RGYUD KYI 'GREL PA MDZES PA'I RGYAN,
DKYIL 'KHOR CHEN PO'I SGRUB THABS SMRi TI'I RANG 'GYUR, SBYIN
SREG GI CHO GA ,RO SREG GI CHO GA ,SLOB DPON YE SHES RDO RJES
MDZAD

PA'I THUGS RJE 'BYUNG BA'I SGOM BZLAS RIN CHEN BZANG PO'I 'GYUR,
SLOB DPON RDO RJE LCAGS KYUS MDZAD PA'I RDO RJE SEMS PA'I YI GE
BRGYA PA'I CHO GA, SLOB DPON ZHI BA SNYING POS MDZAD PA'I RNAL
'BYOR GYI RGYUD DANG MTHUN PA'I MCHOD RTEN SGRUB PA'I CHO GA,

SLOB DPON SANGS RGYAS GSANG BAS MDZAD PA'I RGYUD KYI DON LA 'JUG
PA 'JAM DPAL GO CHA'I 'GYUR, DE'I 'GREL PA SLOB DPON CHEN PO
BADZRAS MDZAD PA, SLOB DPON SHANTI BAS MDZAD PA'I THAMS CAD
GSANG BA'I RGYUD KYI BSHAD SBYAR GSANG BA'I SGRON MA, SLOB

GA ,SLOB DPON SHUDDHI PRA WAS MDZAD PA'I THIG GDAB PA'I RIM PA,

CHO GA, DE'I RANG 'GREL, GTOR MA CHA GSUM 'BRING PO STE, DE
RNAMS RIN CHEN

BZANG PO'I 'GYUR, SLOB DPON DHARMA KI RTIS MDZAD PA'I THIG GI
CHO GA, SLOB DPON MU NI TI TA KO shAS MDZAD PA'I 'JIG RTEN GSUM
LAS RGYAL BA'I 'GREL PA DANG, RDO RJE DBYINGS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR
GYI RNAM GZHAG RIN CHEN BZANG PO'I 'GYUR, NGAN SONG SBYONG BA'I
DKYIL 'KHOR

GYI SGRUB THABS KYI 'GREL PA, DPAL LDAN RGYA CHE'I DKYIL CHOG
,SLOB DPON SKAL BZANG DGA' BAS MDZAD PA'I NGAN SONG SBYONG BA'I
THABS G-YUNG DRUNG 'OD KYI 'GYUR, NGAN SONG SBYONG BA'I CHO GA'I
BYA BA MDOR BSDUS PA, SLOB DPON RATNA KIRTIS MDZAD PA'I SHES RAB
KYI

KYIS MDZAD PA'I SPYOD PA BSDUS PA'I SGRON MA RIN CHEN PHRENG BA
RIN CHEN

THABS SLOB DPON KUN DGA' SNYING PO'I RJES SU 'BRANGS PA, 'DI LO
CHUNG GIS MDZAD PA YIN GYI RGYA GAR MA MA YIN TE, KHA BYANG MED
PAS 'KHRUL PA YIN NO, ,RDO RJE DBYINGS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR KYI DON
BSDUS

GA CHEN PO SLOB DPON RIGS KYIS BYIN PAS MDZAD PA BYA BA BSDUS PA
ZHES BYA BA
